Across the 18 satellites now in orbit, nine clocks have stopped operating."<br /><br />Repairing the Hubble Space Telescope: The Tools Astronauts Used<br /><a href="http://www.space.com/29507-hubble-space-telescope-repair-tools.html" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCMyH88igqdICFSipnAodNMYL6Cj4HQ" data-url="http://www.space.com/29507-hubble-space-telescope-repair-tools.html" data-target-new-window="True" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">http://www.space.com/29507-hubble-spa...</a> <br />"When NASA launched the Hubble Space Telescope on April 24, 1990, the agency already intended to send astronauts up to change out the observatory's scientific instruments from time to time, keeping it at the forefront of science."<br /><br />Kepler's Second Light: How K2 Will Work <br /><a href="https://www.nasa.gov/kepler/keplers-second-light-how-k2-will-work" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCMyH88igqdICFSipnAodNMYL6Cj4HQ" data-url="https://www.nasa.gov/kepler/keplers-second-light-how-k2-will-work" data-target-new-window="True" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://www.nasa.gov/kepler/keplers-s...</a> <br />"In May, Kepler lost the second of four gyroscope-like reaction wheels, ending new data collection for the original mission. A new mission concept, dubbed K2, would continue Kepler's search for other worlds, and introduce new opportunities to observe star clusters, young and old stars, active galaxies and supernovae."<br />____________________<br /><br />DNews is dedicated to satisfying your curiosity and to bringing you mind-bending stories & perspectives you won't find anywhere else!
